#### Prerequisites

##### ‚óΩ - **BST Insert and Remove** - [Data Structures & Algorithms for Beginners](https://neetcode.io/courses/dsa-for-beginners/18)

##### ‚óΩ - **Depth-First Search** - [Data Structures & Algorithms for Beginners](https://neetcode.io/courses/dsa-for-beginners/19)

##### ‚óΩ - **Breadth-First Search** - [Data Structures & Algorithms for Beginners](https://neetcode.io/courses/dsa-for-beginners/20)

##### ‚óΩ - **BST Sets and Maps** - [Data Structures & Algorithms for Beginners](https://neetcode.io/courses/dsa-for-beginners/21)

##### ‚óΩ - **Iterative DFS** - [Advanced Algorithms](https://neetcode.io/courses/advanced-algorithms/9)

### Tries

#### Prerequisites

##### ‚óΩ - **Trie** - [Advanced Algorithms](https://neetcode.io/courses/advanced-algorithms/6)

#### Problems

#### Prerequisites

##### ‚óΩ - **2-Dimension DP** - [Data Structures & Algorithms for Beginners](https://neetcode.io/courses/dsa-for-beginners/33)

##### ‚óΩ - **0 / 1 Knapsack** - [Advanced Algorithms](https://neetcode.io/courses/advanced-algorithms/18)

##### ‚óΩ - **Unbounded Knapsack** - [Advanced Algorithms](https://neetcode.io/courses/advanced-algorithms/19)

##### ‚óΩ - **LCS** - [Advanced Algorithms](https://neetcode.io/courses/advanced-algorithms/20)
